2,  5,  8, 11, 14, 17, ... ^TPEATA4k

Geometric Sequence ^Pal4iKT4

The second term of a geometric sequence is 4 and the 4th term is 8. The common ratio is positive. Find the exact values of:
a) The common ratio
b) The first term
c) The 10th term ^EhhF45oi

The numbers 3, x and x + 6 form the first three terms of a postive geometric sequence. Find:
a) The value of x.
b) The 10th term in the sequence. ^TSsOgxoo

"positive geometric sequence" ^MefCqZvl

What is the first term in the geometric progression 3, 6, 12, 24, ... to exceed 1 million ^3LK1ziYX
